<div id="review_2267236520" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2267236520" />
    <a title="Cindy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57797254-cindy"><img alt="Cindy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598112512p2/57797254.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2267236520?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cindy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cindy" href="/user/show/57797254-cindy">Cindy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2267236520" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18246759449625842571">4.5 stars for a simple yet solid standalone fantasy YA. I devoured this book so quickly and it's the first time I loved reading the enemies-to-lovers trope, because the main characters, their development, their inner fears, and their banter with each other were all done so naturally well. Both protagonists were truly lethal that I wanted to fly through the book just to see how they could possibly even like each other. It’s also fun to see all the different places they went to and how the kingdom</span>
  <span id="freeText18246759449625842571" style="display:none">4.5 stars for a simple yet solid standalone fantasy YA. I devoured this book so quickly and it's the first time I loved reading the enemies-to-lovers trope, because the main characters, their development, their inner fears, and their banter with each other were all done so naturally well. Both protagonists were truly lethal that I wanted to fly through the book just to see how they could possibly even like each other. It’s also fun to see all the different places they went to and how the kingdoms differ from one another; the world building is easy to digest without bogging you down with overcomplicated description and extraneous information. I’m on the fence between giving this 4 or 5 stars because I truly enjoyed reading the characters and their snappy dialogue and I wouldn’t change much else. Really the only nitpick I have is that although the first and last 1/3 of the book is exciting and intriguing, I found the middle portion to be a little meandering, and it was almost too easy to see the characters go from Point A to Point B in their adventure. If we’re going to take this time following the characters in such a linear way, I would’ve liked to see more of the romantic development in order to build up the angst and tension later on. Still, this is pretty much on par with An Enchantment of Ravens as a solid standalone fantasy with good romance to root for.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18246759449625842571" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1599793164" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1599793164" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1599793164?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781471407390" href="/book/show/37541225-to-kill-a-kingdom">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=pirates">pirates</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=epic-fantasy">epic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1599793164" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2462332109878881266"><b>Everything about this book was a salty swashbuckling GLORY and I loved it.</b> I'm alllll here for pirates and sirens and (dark) Little Mermaid retellings, and this just delivered omg. Plus it was super funny, and if there's something my dark little heart beats faster for: it's people who sass each other to death so lovingly.<br/><br/>(Also, claim to fame 😂, I have been a beta-reader for Allie in the past, so I kneeeew I'd love this and ajfdksald her writing is a masterpiece.)<br/><br/><b>+ The characters just stole the s</b></span>
  <span id="freeText2462332109878881266" style="display:none"><b>Everything about this book was a salty swashbuckling GLORY and I loved it.</b> I'm alllll here for pirates and sirens and (dark) Little Mermaid retellings, and this just delivered omg. Plus it was super funny, and if there's something my dark little heart beats faster for: it's people who sass each other to death so lovingly.<br /><br />(Also, claim to fame 😂, I have been a beta-reader for Allie in the past, so I kneeeew I'd love this and ajfdksald her writing is a masterpiece.)<br /><br /><b>+ The characters just stole the seawater ahhh I'm so happy!</b><br />It's dual narrated by both Elian and Lira. Elian is an anti-prince (like "here is a crown but I don't want it) and Lira is a siren (like "here is a prince what if I ate him"). He's hunting her and she's hunting him, which is obviously the recipe for a perfect romance. And their romance was A++ like this is enemies-to-lovers at its finest! It wasn't rushed or awkward. Seriously <i>such</i> perfect fun to see them go from distrust to distant admiration to snarking at each other to "accidentally" "saving" each other's lives. Like YEAH that's no indication of liking of courseeeee, Lira.<br /><br />(Lira was in such denial the whole time. So cute.)<br /><br />I <b>also loved them just as individual characters!</b> Lira is a murderous siren, but also with a soft streak. She takes care of her murder-little-cousin, but she also enjoys the thrill of killing princes. But she totally won my heart too, just by being so complex and compelling. And <b>Elian?!</b> He was the sass pirate of your HEART. I swear. That boy. He was smooth and sassy and absolutely allergic to the idea of being king. Bless him. <br /><br /><b>+ This makes you truly fall in love with the sea too!</b><br />Which is ironic, given that the sea was super deadly but oh well. I love it. I love the descriptions! I could actually <i>see</i> the gorgeous settings, taste the salty sea, and absolutely lose myself in the world. There's plenty of sailing too! And although I KNOW they were all claiming the "pirate" title lol lol Elian you sweetheart. He was a siren killer and really didn't do anything piratey (except for fight with other pirates). But I love pirates. I'll let him have it.<br /><br /><b>+ Like world building gets a hella yes.</b><br />There are SO many different places they went to! Kingdoms and mountains and palaces! It was INCREDIBLY well done too. No getting swamped with mega-long passages of description, yet I could see each setting so clearly. (Plus they were excitingly unique?! With kingdoms of frost and blue-lipped kings, and queendoms of love, with cursed queens on heart thrones.) My opinion is: yes.<br /><br /><b>+ Also it keeps you entertained with sassy banter the whole time.</b><br />This part I truly adored. And smiled a bit like the dork I am. I also loved that Lira/Elian were sassing each other to death, but also the secondary characters were too! Madrid/Kye's banter was amazing!<br /><br /><blockquote>"If the necklace is that precious," I say, "we should have just killed Tallis to get it."<br />"You can't just kill everyone you don't like."<br />"I know that. Otherwise you'd be dead already."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"Remind me not to get on your bad said," Elian says.<br />"Too late."</blockquote><br /><br /><b>+ Was it dark?</b><br />It was very bloody (although not gory) and I would definitely say it's a dark one. So pleased. (I'M NORMAL I SWEAR. DON'T BE WORRIED.)<br /><br /><br /><b>This is definitely the kind of book of sea and ruination that I've been longing for.</b> I'm in loooove. It was perfectly written, with scenery and prose that just leap off the page to DEVOUR YOU (go the siren life) with a fantastic combination of pirates and princes, sirens and curses, and a journey that's always fascinating and fast-paced. With buckets of sass and salt along the way. 😍</span>
  <a data-text-id="2462332109878881266" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2306360555" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2306360555" />
    <a title="High Lady of The Night Court" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court"><img alt="High Lady of The Night Court" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1556501727p2/62560505.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2306360555?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="High Lady of The Night Court" class="user" itemprop="url" name="High Lady of The Night Court" href="/user/show/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court">High Lady of The Night Court</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/62560505-high-lady-of-the-night-court?shelf=retellings-read">retellings-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2306360555" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15360566605437606841"><b>
  <i>Two kingdoms that come with responsibilities we each have trouble bearing. Him, the shackles of being pinned to one land and one life. Me, trapped in the confines of my mother’s murderous legacy. And the ocean, calling out to us both. A song of freedom and longing.</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>I LOVE IT. </i><br/>Reading this book was an amazing experience, I absolutely flew through it. To me this book doesn’t feel like a standalone because I have grown to care for these characters impossibly fast, and I will miss them dearly. Th</span>
  <span id="freeText15360566605437606841" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Two kingdoms that come with responsibilities we each have trouble bearing. Him, the shackles of being pinned to one land and one life. Me, trapped in the confines of my mother’s murderous legacy. And the ocean, calling out to us both. A song of freedom and longing.</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>I LOVE IT. </i><br />Reading this book was an amazing experience, I absolutely flew through it. To me this book doesn’t feel like a standalone because I have grown to care for these characters impossibly fast, and I will miss them dearly. The story was very well written, it didn’t feel rushed, it didn’t feel slow, it had the perfect pace and conveyed exactly want it wanted to say.<br /><br />In this book we follow Lira, the Siren known as Prince’s Bane, and Elian, the prince who is also a Siren killer. We join a human Lira in her attempt to kill Elian and gain the Sea Queen’s favor in order to be turned back into a Siren and a worthy heir to the throne. We join Elian in his attempt to find an object that will help him eliminate Sirenkind once and for all. Both of them are trying to the the exact opposite of what the other wants, which is kind of hilarious, but seeing them contemplate whether what they are doing what it wants is mesmerising.<br /><br />Lira is the heir to the Siren kingdom, she has been pressurised all her life to get rid of her humanity and has been oppressed to become the emotionless, vile creature her mother wants her to be. Elian is a prince, who hates the confines of his duties, and chooses to escape them by becoming a pirate and hunting sirens, with the people he trusts.<br /><br />Every time we are given a glimpse from Lira’s childhood, the torment she is put through because she is the heir to the Sea is truly grievous. A siren, no matter what is still s girl, a child, whose humanity was stolen from her at an age where it would shape her personality for the rest of her life. And watching Lira’s humanity being stripped away from her piece by piece, and by her own mother, is heartbreaking. But as much as it made her a monster, it gave her a sense of responsibility to take what is hers and protect it. <br /><br />Elian’s interactions with his crew are just as endearing. The camaraderie between him and his crew is something to marvel at. Once Lira spends more time around this amazing group of people, none of can deny the tiny spark of humanity that rises in her, however against her wishes. We witness her contemplate that spark and realise the truth of how evil she has become, and that maybe even<i> wanting</i> to be like her mother was wrong.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>The truth of what I am has become a nightmare.</i>
</b><br /><br />More than anything we slowly realise that there are small things in their lives, which they have either found or created to find solace in. Elian finds that solace in being with his crew, the family he chose who are the people he can truly be himself with. And Lira in all her savageness she chose to protect her cousin, the one person she saw an innocence in worth protecting. Without even knowing it, by protecting her cousin Lira was protecting not only a spark of innocence, but also the part of her that is human enough to choose love and kindness over the monster her mother wanted her to become.<br /><br />We see both of them run from the people they were forced to become because of the position they were born in, we see them resent the people they were raised to be and find them fighting their way out of the moulds society carved for them. <br />This is a story of a girl and a boy pushed to be people they don’t want to be. A story of how they choose the be the people they want to be and watching them grow to realize who they really want to be is an amazing experience. I highly recommend it and if you are thinking of reading this book I urge you to read it. <br />I mean come on you can't possibly go wrong with pirates! And believe me when I say we've gone a <b>long </b>way from Little Mermaid.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15360566605437606841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_2321249712" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2321249712" />
    <a title="Camila Roy ••RoyIsReading••" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40788320-camila-roy-royisreading"><img alt="Camila Roy ••RoyIsReading••" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532282247p2/40788320.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2321249712?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Camila Roy ••RoyIsReading••" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Camila Roy ••RoyIsReading••" href="/user/show/40788320-camila-roy-royisreading">Camila Roy ••RoyIsReading••</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40788320-camila-roy-royisreading?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2321249712" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9440821421868961038">RATING: 5/5<br/><br/><b>I LOVED THIS BOOK!!</b> Is it weird that I am obssessed with the two main characters? They're fkn murderers! I don't think that's ever happened before. <br/><br/>It's not my style to include synopsis in my reviews, but I'll make an exception just this once because I really want others to read it. We got two POVs in this story: The first is from a siren princess that kills human princes. The second one is from a human prince that kills sirens. Their paths cross and...you'll have to find out the rest</span>
  <span id="freeText9440821421868961038" style="display:none">RATING: 5/5<br /><br /><b>I LOVED THIS BOOK!!</b> Is it weird that I am obssessed with the two main characters? They're fkn murderers! I don't think that's ever happened before. <br /><br />It's not my style to include synopsis in my reviews, but I'll make an exception just this once because I really want others to read it. We got two POVs in this story: The first is from a siren princess that kills human princes. The second one is from a human prince that kills sirens. Their paths cross and...you'll have to find out the rest for yourself ??<br /><br />This was one of my most anticipated reads of the year and I'm sooo glad it didn't disappoint. Once I started I could not stop. It felt so real, which is ironic because it's a fantasy. Something about Lira and Elian was addicting and I couldn't get enough. <br /><br />I do have a couple of complains, though. The big reveal (when one of the characters found out about the other's identity) was too simple. I don't know what I was expecting, honestly. Maybe a little more yelling? Or just a heated argument? Whatever, I can overlook that part. However, Elian's decision at the end is kind of hard to process. Maybe I'm just used to fantasy characters being overly complicated and I can't settle for simplicity.<br /> <br />Best thing about this book? The EPIC plot. I don't have much experience reading retellings but I definitely felt a Little Mermaid vibe from this. Mission accomplished, autor!<br /><br />In conclussion, this is definitely a favorite of the month and possibly of the year. Was it worth the wait? YES. Would I recommend it? YESSSS!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9440821421868961038" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2309357723" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2309357723" />
    <a title="Angelica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16201093-angelica"><img alt="Angelica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507050077p2/16201093.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2309357723?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angelica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angelica" href="/user/show/16201093-angelica">Angelica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=a-good-pair">a-good-pair</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=cool-tittle">cool-tittle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=fairytales">fairytales</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=great-ending">great-ending</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16201093-angelica?shelf=awesome-heroines">awesome-heroines</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2309357723" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3418762254136897656">You guys! Go read this book! It was so good. Like, sooooo good and I just finished reading it like ten minutes ago and I'm dying right now. <b>And AAAAAAAHHHHHH</b>, I literally can't even! Seriously though. <b>UUUGGHHHH!!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418946978ra/12952774.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But anyway, now that I got my incoherent rambling out of the way, let's talk about this book and the fact that I loved it. <br/><br/>This here isn't your typical Little Mermaid retelling. There's no sweet princess with romantic ideas about the human world. No innocent prince looking for love.<br/><br/>Inst</span>
  <span id="freeText3418762254136897656" style="display:none">You guys! Go read this book! It was so good. Like, sooooo good and I just finished reading it like ten minutes ago and I'm dying right now. <b>And AAAAAAAHHHHHH</b>, I literally can't even! Seriously though. <b>UUUGGHHHH!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418946978ra/12952774.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But anyway, now that I got my incoherent rambling out of the way, let's talk about this book and the fact that I loved it. <br><br>This here isn't your typical Little Mermaid retelling. There's no sweet princess with romantic ideas about the human world. No innocent prince looking for love.<br><br>Instead, we get Lira, a cruel siren princess who takes pleasure in ripping the hearts of princes right out of their drowning bodies. We also get Elian, a daring young prince who has devoted his life to hunting and killing sirens.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Technically, I'm a murderer, but I like to think that's one of my better qualities."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>They are both rough around the edges, both willing to do whatever they deem necessary, and both unafraid to get their hands a little bloody. When fate thrusts them together what we get is a book worth of verbal battles as they use their wit to draw each other out. We get tension and action, we get slowly building friendships and even slower building romances. Basically, we get a lot of awesome things that you are just gonna have to see for yourself.<br><br>The author's writing style is truly beautiful. It's fluid and enchanting and I cannot wait to see what else she writes in the future because I'm officially a fan. I loved how she wrote the narrative and especially how she wrote the dialogue between characters. You could tell how close they all were and how their relationships were built. <b>And the conversations between Lira and Elian were absolutely golden!</b><br><br>The characters themselves were equally magnificent. Yes, Lira and Elian were amazing,  we know that, but it wasn't just them, it was everyone else too. All of the characters we meet are fleshed out, well-rounded characters. They have wants and needs and personalities that don't revolve around just making the plot happen. Basically what I'm saying is that they were all real characters and not just convenient plot devices, and I loved them all.<br><br>Then there was the world in which this story took place. It was unique and intriguing. I loved the way the author incorporated so many different myths into the story, seamlessly weaving them into her world without distracting from the main storyline. For example, Midas myth with the city of gold was great, as were the myths of the other royal families.  Also, just putting this out here, <b>this world was extremely diverse!</b> You really do get the sense that it's a whole world being created, not just the stereotypical, magical version of England or France or some other big European country that we've all grown uncomfortably accustomed to in YA fantasy.<br><br>Overall, I really liked this book, in case you hadn't yet noticed. But, all my gushing aside, this was an extremely well written, highly imaginative retelling, and it was so much better than I ever thought it would be.<br><br>My one complaint, because I wouldn't be me if I didn't complain about something, is that the chapters weren't labeled. The book had dual POV and it didn't always evenly alternate between Lira and Elian, so sometimes I would get to the third paragraph in a chapter before I realized which character I was reading from. Other than that, I must say kudos to you, Alexandra Christo. This was one heck of a debut.<br><br>**I received an advance copy of this book from the publisher via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. All opinions are my own.**<br><br>This review first appeared on <a href="https://thebookcovergirls.wordpress.com/2018/02/28/to-kill-a-kingdom-the-retelling-ive-been-waiting-for/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Cover Girl blog</a>.<br><br>Follow Me Here Too:<b> <a href="http://www.thebookcovergirls.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">My Blog</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/covergirlreads" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/book-cover-girl-19339391" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin'</a> || <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookcovergirls//" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://thebookcovergirls.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/thebookcovergirls/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13643040990892365561">remember when i said this book was good?? well it is, but you know what, the more i think about it, the more i've realized that the ending was anticlimatic as fuck and Lira and Elian's relationship can choke on balls the size of my pEn!!!!<br/><br/>i guess i really hyped this up and ended up giving it 4 stars in a rush because i was really enjoying it <i>in the moment</i>, but once the ending came and i actually used my brain to think about it, i was like hMmMmMmMmmmm NO THIS IS KIND OF A PIECE OF SHIT!!!!<br/><br/>LET'S </span>
  <span id="freeText13643040990892365561" style="display:none">remember when i said this book was good?? well it is, but you know what, the more i think about it, the more i've realized that the ending was anticlimatic as fuck and Lira and Elian's relationship can choke on balls the size of my pEn!!!!<br><br>i guess i really hyped this up and ended up giving it 4 stars in a rush because i was really enjoying it <i>in the moment</i>, but once the ending came and i actually used my brain to think about it, i was like hMmMmMmMmmmm NO THIS IS KIND OF A PIECE OF SHIT!!!!<br><br>LET'S TALK ABOUT WHY IT'S ENJOYABLE!!!!<br><br>first off, this has such an interesting plot. a killer siren princess who rips the hearts out of princey boys to represent her age(??). but then little ruthless Lira fucked up and abusive piece of shit mommy got really mad and turned her into a! human! and that's like,,, very humiliating in the siren world, and on the land, our prince/pirate boy Elian kills sirens. one day on his ship, he sees a woman floating in the sea and decides to help her. le shock, it <s>issa me, mArIo</s> is Lira!!!! <s>
  <b>and that's how killer siren/human hybrid babies are made</b>
</s>. and so she decides to help him on his quest and whatever!!!<br><br>what i love so much about these two characters is how they always have a witty comeback prepared for anything the other person says and it's like an indirect challenge to leave the other person speechless by roasting tf out of them. THAT IS THE TYPE OF CONTENT I NEVER KNEW I WANTED. and i got it from lira and elian sjkfbqdw. they're so fucking funnyyy!!! and lira being clueless about many everyday human things added on to the comedic aspect. i genuinely found myself laughing.<br><br>also, elian's crew is GOALS AF. they're funny, strong, loyal, loving and so protective towards each other. they always got each others backs their friendships are just so pure and wholesome!!!<br><br>THE FEMALE CHARACTERS BLEW ME AWAY WITH DAT BADASSERY !! the princess, the girl on elian's crew and lira and some of the other woman are so fucking brutal and badass, someone pick me up because holy shit, it was fine af <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526164865ra/25529399.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>also, there's a lot of death, and brutal murdering, it's great, you should read it! :)<br><br><u>NOW ON TO SHIT I FUCKING DESPISE:</u><br><br>something about the writing and world building felt very lacking and monotonous. the action scenes also, felt really not as intense as they should have been. like, the writing is just MONOTONOUS !!<br><br><b>L I R A A N D E L I A N SITTING IN A TREE, NO K I S S I N G BECAUSE THEIR RELATIONSHIP SUCKED ASS AND THEY WERE BETTER OFF AS FRIENDS. </b><br><br>THEY WERE DOING SO WELL AND THEN YA HAD TO GO OFF AND MAKE IT A SHIT ROMANCE SLKWQDKSBVDSKLAVA, NO.<br><br>FUC<br>K<br><br>THEM.<br><br>ALSO WHAT THE FRICKITY FRACK WAS THAT ANTICLIMATIC ENDING. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[EVERYTHING GOT RESOLVED SO EASILY AND THEN IT'S JUST A HAPPILY EVER AFTER, UM NO, BITVH. WHAT THE FUCK <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>[rage quits and dies]</b><br><br>buddy read with my girl <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/67405281-yusra" rel="nofollow noopener">Yusra</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2268126139" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2268126139" />
    <a title="Sabrina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/63480503-sabrina"><img alt="Sabrina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600832447p2/63480503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2268126139?book_show_action=true">Feb 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/63480503-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/63480503-sabrina?shelf=almost-favorites">almost-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2268126139" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18180136917015021427"><i>
  <b>“His face makes no difference.” I drop her hand. “It’s his heart I’m after.”<br/>“So many hearts.” Her voice is angelic. “You’ll soon run out of room to bury them all.”<br/>I lick my lips. “Maybe,” I say. “But a princess must have her prince.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/>This book is so unique and fun to read.<br/>SIRENS 🧜‍♀️ and PIRATES, just how freaking awesome is that?!? <br/>I have an unhealthy obsession with sirens and pirates 🤪<br/><br/>Lira and Elian are awesome, funny, sarcastic, intelligent and badass. I love the dynamic that they have and</span>
  <span id="freeText18180136917015021427" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“His face makes no difference.” I drop her hand. “It’s his heart I’m after.”<br />“So many hearts.” Her voice is angelic. “You’ll soon run out of room to bury them all.”<br />I lick my lips. “Maybe,” I say. “But a princess must have her prince.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />This book is so unique and fun to read.<br />SIRENS 🧜‍♀️ and PIRATES, just how freaking awesome is that?!? <br />I have an unhealthy obsession with sirens and pirates 🤪<br /><br />Lira and Elian are awesome, funny, sarcastic, intelligent and badass. I love the dynamic that they have and the relationship development was fantastic.<br /><i>
  <b>“We are not naïve little heirs to be molded as they wish. We are warriors. We are rulers”</b>
</i><br /><br />The villain of the story was great and real and really after all a freaking villain to the core!!!<br /><i>
  <b>“She is a performer as much as she is a queen.”</b>
</i><br /><br />The side characters are amazing and the friendships are so funny.<br /><br />And how they didn’t try to justify every bad thing they did and they forgive each other is just life💘.<br /><br />The writing, literally everything was just on point in this one!! <br /><br />I had all of my questions answered, and for a single book, a lot happened and all made bloody sense. Which may be hard to find in a standalone. <br /><br />One scene in particular that I can’t really say (spoiler) just made me so happy 😍😁. I was smiling so hard. It was just an entertaining read!!<br /><i>
  <b>“I smile at that, because Elian of all people should know better. He should know to have more faith in myth and fairy tale”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />BR with Ronak(Pihu) Gajjar💕.</span>

<div id="review_2280220891" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2280220891" />
    <a title="lily ☁️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10148904-lily"><img alt="lily ☁️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517405104p2/10148904.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2280220891?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="lily ☁️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="lily ☁️" href="/user/show/10148904-lily">lily ☁️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36120821-to-kill-a-kingdom">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=to-reread">to-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=tolino">tolino</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=best-romance">best-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10148904-lily?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2280220891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer296825952568218515"><blockquote>✨ <b>You can now find my full review <a href='https://sprinklesofdreams.wordpress.com/2018/05/19/book-review-to-kill-a-kingdom-by-alexandra-christo/' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a>!</b> ✨</blockquote><br/>I finished reading this <i>very</i> hyped book—and I wasn’t crippled by disappointment? To quote <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508-maymay-semi-hiatus' rel='nofollow noopener'>May</a>: “<b>omg, lily liking a popular book?? is the world still spinning??</b>” It <i>may</i> have stopped for a second, or two.<br/><br/>But, in all seriousness, <b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34499221.To_Kill_a_Kingdom' title='To Kill a Kingdom by Alexandra Christo' rel='nofollow noopener'>To Kill a Kingdom</a> is brilliant.</b><br/><br/>Don’t get me wrong, it’s not <i>perfect</i> by all means; in fact, I found the initial chapters that introduce us to the world of sirens, mermaids, and the Sea, as well as the world above water with its vario</span>
  <span id="freeText296825952568218515" style="display:none"><blockquote>✨ <b>You can now find my full review <a href="https://sprinklesofdreams.wordpress.com/2018/05/19/book-review-to-kill-a-kingdom-by-alexandra-christo/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>!</b> ✨</blockquote><br />I finished reading this <i>very</i> hyped book—and I wasn’t crippled by disappointment? To quote <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/49148508-maymay-semi-hiatus" rel="nofollow noopener">May</a>: “<b>omg, lily liking a popular book?? is the world still spinning??</b>” It <i>may</i> have stopped for a second, or two.<br /><br />But, in all seriousness, <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34499221.To_Kill_a_Kingdom" title="To Kill a Kingdom by Alexandra Christo" rel="nofollow noopener">To Kill a Kingdom</a> is brilliant.</b><br /><br />Don’t get me wrong, it’s not <i>perfect</i> by all means; in fact, I found the initial chapters that introduce us to the world of sirens, mermaids, and the Sea, as well as the world above water with its various kingdoms, a bit dull at times—and I was afraid I’d end up resenting this book.<br /><br />But much like an avalanche gaining speed, power, and force as it nears the bottom of the slope, I slowly came to be completely enraptured with it, as it turned more and more action-packed, volatile, and grand in every way.<br /><br /><i>To Kill a Kingdom</i> is in its essence a retelling of the fairytale <i>The Little Mermaid</i>, but the only elements of the story that are adopted from it are that a sea creature is turned into a human girl by an evil witch, and her fate hinges on whether or not she manages to fulfill the witch’s quest. Only, in this book’s case, it’s not a mermaid that is cursed, but a deadly siren, and the evil witch is her mother, the Sea Queen.<br /><br />Our heroine Lira, a royal siren, and daughter of the Sea Queen, is nothing like the sweet, innocent, gullible Arielle in the fairytale. She’s fierce, ruthless, and bloodthirsty.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I can’t help but be mesmerized. Such beautiful creatures. Such bewitching, deadly things. Even as they sharpen their fangs on their lips and run taloned hands through their liquid hair, I can’t look away. Everything about them is awful, but nothing about them is hideous.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Through an unfortunate turn of events, she mistakenly saves Prince Elian instead of killing him by stealing his heart, and so her mother punishes her by turning her into a human girl.<br /><br />I was honestly so impressed by the development of Elian and Lira’s relationship—the tenuous (mis-)trust, the banter, and the initial aversion between them—it was very believable, well-paced, and most significantly, I found myself rooting for them.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“It feels like the worst thing I’ve ever done and the best thing I could ever do and how strange that the two are suddenly the same. How strange that instead of taking his heart, I’m hoping he takes mine.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34499221.To_Kill_a_Kingdom" title="To Kill a Kingdom by Alexandra Christo" rel="nofollow noopener">To Kill a Kingdom</a> does feel like a debut novel at times, but it somehow only served to reinforce the positive impression it made on me. It was both darker, but also funnier than I expected—it comprised so many clever puns (which I’m a sucker for) and witty banter, and it featured immensely rounded characters who were snarky, and endearing, as well as great relationships (bless the bromance in this book).<br /><br /><b>I’m so happy that such a hyped book for <i>once</i> worked out for me.</b><br /><br /><a href="https://sprinklesofdreams.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="http://twitter.com/sprnklsofdreams" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/sprinklesofdreamsx/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://sprinklesofdreams.tumblr.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.bloglovin.com/blogs/sprinkles-dreams-19449885" rel="nofollow noopener">Bloglovin’</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="296825952568218515" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2217784499" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2217784499" />
    <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader"><img alt="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579173421p2/43850323.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2217784499?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader">Reynita Maharani ★ The Night Reader ★</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781471407390" href="/book/show/37541225-to-kill-a-kingdom">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=bored-me-to-death">bored-me-to-death</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=what-the-hell-is-this">what-the-hell-is-this</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=boring-romance">boring-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=ya-books">ya-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=didn-t-live-up-my-expectations">didn-t-live-up-my-expectations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=fantasy-books">fantasy-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=retelling-books">retelling-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=romance-books">romance-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2217784499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11998462177961044758"><b>THE REVIEW IS POSTED<br/><br/>2.7 STARS </b> <br/><br/>I honestly don't know where to begin. This book disappointed me very much and it's not like I had high expectations before reading it, in fact my expectations before reading it were pretty low because I didn't know what to expect and I just wanted to read it. I thought that at least this would be a 3 star read for me but nope, that didn't happen or maybe this book just isn't a cup of my tea. <br/><br/>To be honest, I rarely read books about sirens or pirates and I don't know</span>
  <span id="freeText11998462177961044758" style="display:none"><b>THE REVIEW IS POSTED<br /><br />2.7 STARS </b> <br /><br />I honestly don't know where to begin. This book disappointed me very much and it's not like I had high expectations before reading it, in fact my expectations before reading it were pretty low because I didn't know what to expect and I just wanted to read it. I thought that at least this would be a 3 star read for me but nope, that didn't happen or maybe this book just isn't a cup of my tea. <br /><br />To be honest, I rarely read books about sirens or pirates and I don't know why, those aren't really my favorites but if the stories were good or seemed good for me, then I would definitely read them and I read this book because they synopsis sounded good and I was intrigued to know more about the book and I wish I didn't read this book. <i>
  <b>I fucking wasted my time.</b>
</i><br /><br />There were some parts that I liked in this book though ( thankfully! ). <br /><br />❤ I liked how brutal and scary it was. It was pretty scary and interesting to read and this book was good enough if I only thought about how scary and brutal it was. <br />❤ The secondary characters! omg I really liked Madrid and Kye. They were such good characters and They were <b>A LOT</b> more interesting than Lira or Elian. Madrid and Kye made me laugh or grinned several times and they were also cute and I liked them so much! <br /><br />What I did not like :<br /><br />☹ The pacing of the book was really slow. I love slow pacing books but THAT WAS TOO SLOW and I was bored. I kept reading it because I was still patient enough and I still wanted to know more about the book BUT OH MY GOD, THIS BOOK WAS SO SLOW and I did not have the patience anymore to read it so I skimmed reading it when I reached page 214. <br /><br />☹ This book was fucking boring. I swear, I almost always fell asleep or felt sleepy when I read this book. ( except when Madrid or Kye made me laugh or when the book scared me ) <br />There were actions scenes in this book but they just didn't hold my interest. The book was just boring and when I read this book time moved so slow and I just couldn't read fast enough and it frustrated me! because I just wanted to finish reading this book. That's all I wanted. <br /><br />☹ I don't know what to say about Elian and Lira. They were not plain but they were not interesting either. The only characters that I cared were Madrid and Kye. I didn't care about Elian and Lira. <br /><br />☹ I can't say much about the romance other than I didn't care about it and I also didn't feel anything toward the romance. <br /><br /><b>Basically, I am just so disappointed right now and I wasted my time reading it.</b> <br /><br />••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br /><br /><b> <br />Me : *holds the book and whispers to it* <br />Me : Goodbye. I will never miss you. <br /><br /><s>REVIEW TO COME SOON.</s> <br /><br /></b> <br />••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••<br /><br /><b>After not reading a book for several days, I AM FINALLY READING A BOOK AGAIN! YAY! Have you guys read this book? And what do you think of it? (no spoiler please ) 😊<br /></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11998462177961044758" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2140211318" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2140211318" />
    <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance"><img alt="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513125058p2/68538597.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2140211318?book_show_action=true">Apr 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="❄️BooksofRadiance❄️" href="/user/show/68538597-booksofradiance">❄️BooksofRadiance❄️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68538597-booksofradiance?shelf=ya-fantasy-sci-fi">ya-fantasy-sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2140211318" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18445575377390287413">2.5⭐️<br/><br/>This was one of my most anticipated reads of 2018 but for some reason I still went in with some doubts, and I have to say, I was pleasantly surprised -for the most part-.<br/><br/>If I could sum this up in one word it’d be - fun. That’s it, it was a fun and engaging read that had its ups as well as downs. <br/>It would’ve also been a sold 4-star read had it not been for the unnecessary, far fetched romance that completely ruined the entire narrative for me. <br/><br/><b>Starting off with what I liked:</b><br/><br/>✨The sirens:<br/><br/>Damn,</span>
  <span id="freeText18445575377390287413" style="display:none">2.5⭐️<br /><br />This was one of my most anticipated reads of 2018 but for some reason I still went in with some doubts, and I have to say, I was pleasantly surprised -for the most part-.<br /><br />If I could sum this up in one word it’d be - fun. That’s it, it was a fun and engaging read that had its ups as well as downs. <br />It would’ve also been a sold 4-star read had it not been for the unnecessary, far fetched romance that completely ruined the entire narrative for me. <br /><br /><b>Starting off with what I liked:</b><br /><br />✨The sirens:<br /><br />Damn, I loved how dark and vile they were. I don’t like retellings and I also don’t like children’s books -Disney and whatnot-, they’re not the sort of books I grew up reading; I didn’t like them when I was a child myself and I certainly don’t like them now so I had a very restricted knowledge of the Little Mermaid story going in. Thus, for me this was refreshing. They were just deliciously dark and sinister which I had a joyous time reading. <br /><br />✨How Lira and Elian started off:<br /><br />The other thing I loved was how unrelenting and ruthless both Lira and Elian were, at least at the beginning. They were both sharp-witted and set in their ways to accomplish whatever messed up goals they had: Lira, to kill and take the prince’s heart and Elian, to rid the world of sirens. At least, that was the case...😒<br />- I also loved the banter and snark between all of the characters, not just Lira &amp; Elian. It was as if they were incapable of having a straightforward conversation. Each comment was met with an equally snarky and snide comeback, and I was here for it. <br /><br /><b>Now to the dreaded drawbacks, (had to be done).</b><br /><br />✨The unnecessary, unrealistic, unreasonable romance. That’s right. 🤦‍♀️<br /><br />I get it. This is YA and in YA, the term platonic does not exist. All roads have to lead back to a bloody romance! I’m sick of it.<br />I just don’t get it; where, in what (stupid) rule book, does it say that two people who start off as strangers have to end up as lovers!? Why not end as comrades? As friends? Or even stay enemies while helping one another further their personal agenda? <br /><br />This could and would have been a fantastic book if it hadn’t been ruined by their sudden newfound “love” for each other. All that ruthlessness, from both characters, that I was so attracted to instantly dissipated the moment they started getting all weak and sappy (I am, by no means, saying romance makes you weak but some semblance of believability makes all the difference).<br />I was promised a ruthless siren and relentless prince on a murdering rampage - obviously, not the case here at all. <br /><br />✨Lira’s change of heart: <br /><br />This’s a continuation to what I’ve just said above but for whatever reason, I found her change of heart even more irksome than I did Elian’s. <br />She’s born a siren. Raised as a siren and was only a human for, what, just a few days? So, what, that’s all it takes to change one’s nature? Just a few days for her to suddenly forget everything she’s known, her very nature as a siren and grow human emotions? Again, I’m not saying these are bad, not for a human. But not in this particular situation, with a siren. <br /><br />✨Elian’s crusade: <br /><br />This, I had the biggest problem with. <br />I had such a hard time believing his crusade as the saviour of humanity, as “the deadly siren hunter”. <br /><br />Here’s the thing, yes, sirens are deadly in this world BUT not exactly deadly enough to have all the neighbouring kingdoms come together and “fight the big fight” because unless you invade their space which obviously is the seas, they pretty much can’t do anything to you or your land. <br />Even his father, the king, doesn’t really take Elian’s crusade as seriously and only considers it a sort of, ‘get this adventure out of your system before you take the throne’ kind of a thing. So, for me it felt almost like a child’s play. There was just no urgency to it. It wasn’t like the world was going to cease to exist if Elian didn’t “stop the sirens”. <br /><br />Aside from these tiny issues, great, great read. Really. 👍</span>
  <a data-text-id="18445575377390287413" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2191012496" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2191012496" />
    <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries"><img alt="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557144778p2/15335689.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2191012496?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]" href="/user/show/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries">destiny ♡⚔♡ [howling libraries]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=owned-physical">owned-physical</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=owned-ebooks">owned-ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=found-families">found-families</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=review-copies">review-copies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=otp">otp</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=the-best-of-the-best">the-best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15335689-destiny-howling-libraries?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2191012496" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4675874731286382604">Let me say, first and foremost, that I am such a total sucker for books revolving around the ocean, whether it involves pirates, mermaids, sirens, sea creatures, or any mix of those things. When I first heard about this story of a vicious siren chasing down a pirate prince who slays her kind, it skyrocketed to the top of my list of most anticipated releases for 2018. I had every gut feeling in the world that I was going to positively adore this novel, and as you’ll see in my review, I was <i>not</i> di</span>
  <span id="freeText4675874731286382604" style="display:none">Let me say, first and foremost, that I am such a total sucker for books revolving around the ocean, whether it involves pirates, mermaids, sirens, sea creatures, or any mix of those things. When I first heard about this story of a vicious siren chasing down a pirate prince who slays her kind, it skyrocketed to the top of my list of most anticipated releases for 2018. I had every gut feeling in the world that I was going to positively adore this novel, and as you’ll see in my review, I was <i>not</i> disappointed.<br /><br /><blockquote>It’s the princes who hold the allure. In their youth. In the allegiance of their people. In the promise of the leader they could one day become. They are the next generation of rules, and by killing them, I kill the future. Just as my mother taught me.</blockquote><br /><b>→ Lira ←</b><br />While the story alternates between two perspectives, the first one that we are introduced to is Lira, also known as the <i>Prince’s Bane</i> for her cruel slayings of princes. As the daughter of the Sea Queen, her task is to rip the still-beating heart from one prince on each of her birthdays. My favorite thing about Lira, right off the bat, was the fact that she wasn’t some gooey, sweet young girl on the inside; she is unapologetically vicious and coldhearted, which we quickly see is the end result of a lifetime of abuse from her mother.<br /><br /><blockquote> Technically, I’m a murderer, but I like to think that’s one of my better qualities.</blockquote><br />Lira’s interactions with Elian, once she finds herself stranded on his pirate ship, are the definition of enemies-to-lovers behavior: she’s feisty, angry, mean, and conniving, without ever going overboard enough to become genuinely unlikeable. The fact that she has such a difficult home life awaiting her under the sea makes it hard to view her as an outright “villain”, and at many times, I found myself struggling to determine who I wanted to root for: the cutthroat siren, or the vengeance-seeking prince.<br /><br /><blockquote> In my heart, I’m as wild as the ocean that raised me.</blockquote><br /><b>→ Prince Elian ←</b><br />Early in the story, we learn that Lira isn’t the only one trying to live up to their parents’ expectations; while Elian’s family wants him to embrace the kingdom and his future throne, all the young prince wants is his ship, his crew, and the ocean breeze in his sails. I have a total soft spot for these sorts of pirates, whose days are filled less with pillaging and plundering, and more with adventures, heists, and a healthy appreciation for families that are composed not of blood, but of loyalty and friendship. Elian is the single most lovable pirate lord I’ve ever read about, and his crew is an extension of that. They are so fun, snarky, and loyal to a fault.<br /><br /><blockquote> Royalty cannot be unmade. Birth rights cannot be changed. Hearts are forever scarred by our true nature.</blockquote><br />Much like I enjoyed the three-dimensionality of Lira’s spiky exterior, I loved the fact that Elian could have so easily been degraded to a run-of-the-mill “good guy”, but is instead a fantastic antihero. He’s clever, a little callous, and capable of fantastic scheming and thievery. He’s a prince, and arguably the lesser of the evils in this batch of characters, but the author never lets us forget that he is still a <i>pirate</i> – not a hero. (I’d also like to take a moment to point out here that Elian is either black or biracial – we know that his father is black, but his mother’s ethnicity is never confirmed, as far as I recall – which I thought was a fantastic reprieve from the stereotypical “Prince Eric”-inspired guy in stories like this.)<br /><br /><blockquote> “I’d be flattered,” I say, “that you would look for an excuse just to hold my hand.”<br />“Perhaps I’m just looking for an excuse to shoot you.”</blockquote><br /><b>→ romance ←</b><br />There are three things that I absolutely never get tired of in romantic subplots: 1) good, witty banter, 2) enemies-to-lovers tropes, and 3) slow burns. This book checks all three of those boxes <i>magnificently.</i> The back-and-forth chatter between Lira and Elian is so fun and sharp, and the way they shift from distrust and a touch of loathing to something more is so delightful to watch. I was rooting so hard for both of them not only to succeed, but to find a way to succeed <i>together.</i> Best of all, this particular dose of enemies-to-lovers doesn’t breach into abuse territory or a gross power imbalance, as these tropes are so prone to falling into in a lot of YA/NA titles.<br /><br /><blockquote> Every queen began as a siren, and when the crown passed to her, its magic stole her fins and left in their place mighty tentacles that held the strength of armies.</blockquote><br /><b>→ sea lore ←</b><br />I don’t think I could pick just one favorite thing about this story, but if I had to make a list of the traits that would tie for first place, the lore would absolutely make it into that tie. The sirens aren’t depicted as some frail, beautiful creatures; while gorgeous, they’re otherworldly, haunting, wild, fanged things who show no mercy and are powerful enough to wipe out grown men with a single blow. The mermaids are differentiated solidly from the sirens, as inhuman, grotesque creatures with unhinged jaws and bizarre bodies – they’re fabulously creepy and dark, and I loved every single interaction with them.<br /><br /><blockquote>The truth of what I am has become a nightmare.</blockquote><br />While this story never feels like a simple retelling, there’s one aspect that definitely paid homage to some very old and well-known stories, and that is the Sea Queen. The backstory given explains that the power of becoming queen turns sirens into these terrifying, tentacled beings that are incredibly powerful and magical. Lira’s own mother wields her power with pure brutality, and while I won’t spoil for you the curse she places upon her daughter, it’s a delightful twist on the classic tale and made me downright giddy.<br /><br /><blockquote> I’ve become so used to being brutal, that I almost forget it didn’t begin as a choice.</blockquote><br /><b>→ final thoughts ←</b><br />As I mentioned in the preface of this review, <i>To Kill a Kingdom</i> was, hands down, one of my most anticipated releases of 2018, and not a single sentence of it disappointed me. I was captivated from the very first page, and am so delighted to have been granted the opportunity to read it early. I buddy read it with a few friends, who I’ll link to below, and if it tells you anything about how wonderful this story was, every single one of us 5-starred this book at the end of the reading. I think I was only a few chapters into the ARC when I pre-ordered my finished copy, because this is a beautiful stand-alone that I could easily see myself picking up over and over again.<br /><br /><b>Content warnings:</b> abuse, violence, murder, self-harm, sexual harassment.<br /><br /><i>All quotes are taken from an unfinished ARC and may differ from the final publication. Thank you to Feiwel &amp; Friends for providing me with this ARC in exchange for an honest review!</i><br /><br />You can find this review and more on my <a href="https://howlinglibraries.com/2018/03/03/to-kill-a-kingdom/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>, or you can follow me on <a href="https://twitter.com/howlinglibrary" rel="nofollow noopener">twitter</a>, <a href="https://instagram.com/howlinglibraries" rel="nofollow noopener">bookstagram</a>, or <a href="https://facebook.com/howlinglibraries" rel="nofollow noopener">facebook</a>!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4675874731286382604" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69838582-theburqaavenger?shelf=when-life-gives-you-lemons">when-life-gives-you-lemons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69838582-theburqaavenger?shelf=retellings">retellings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69838582-theburqaavenger?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2351190123" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10057900927105504970"><b>A pirate prince <s>who wears eyeliner O H M Y G O O D N E S S</s></b><br/>.<br/>.<br/>.<br/>#sorrynotsorry.<br/><br/>In all seriousness <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34499221.To_Kill_a_Kingdom' title='To Kill a Kingdom by Alexandra Christo' rel='nofollow noopener'>To Kill a Kingdom</a> is brilliant. Yes it does feel like a debut at times but THAT is what forced me appreciate all the others aspects of this book. It was dark (i like), it was funny (i love), it was enemies to lovers (my heart), it has bromance (kill me now), it has amazing banter (gah!), it has a whole pirate crew (*dreamy sighs*), it has sirens (seriously) and it has <b>Elian (my husband) who is also a p</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10057900927105504970" style="display:none"><b>A pirate prince <s>who wears eyeliner O H M Y G O O D N E S S</s></b><br />.<br />.<br />.<br />#sorrynotsorry.<br /><br />In all seriousness <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34499221.To_Kill_a_Kingdom" title="To Kill a Kingdom by Alexandra Christo" rel="nofollow noopener">To Kill a Kingdom</a> is brilliant. Yes it does feel like a debut at times but THAT is what forced me appreciate all the others aspects of this book. It was dark (i like), it was funny (i love), it was enemies to lovers (my heart), it has bromance (kill me now), it has amazing banter (gah!), it has a whole pirate crew (*dreamy sighs*), it has sirens (seriously) and it has <b>Elian (my husband) who is also a pirate prince.</b><br /><br />Our heroine is blood thirsty and ruthless. Our hero is ... *whispers* i am a goner. Honestly i am impressed by the way the author handled their relationship it was s l o w b u r n - it was believable, it was fast-paced and most importantly the author makes you root for them. Some one in the heavens must have been busy because damn the banter in this book is so witty and their were so many clever puns (i am a sucker for good puns). There is so much sass my shipper heart felt so happy.<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Elian says. “When I marry, it won’t be about power.”<br />“What will it be, then?”<br />“Sacrifice.”<br />“You’re right,” I tell him, trying to shake the melancholy from my voice. “Spending a lifetime with you would be a sacrifice.”<br />“Oh?...What would you be losing?” he asks.<br />“If I married you?” I stand to tower above him, pushing away the unraveling thing inside me. “I suppose it would be my mind.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />This is true love guys. If that doesn't capture your attention here is another one:<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“How strange that instead of taking his heart, I'm hoping he takes mine.”<br /></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />.<br />.<br />.<br />yeah.<br /><br />Honestly my only problem is that ending ... seriously?! This was perfect in all other aspects and then that ending happened and my rating dropped :(<br /><br />Anyways, I absolutely LOVED the world-building. gah! This book is action packed. It's fast paced. It's a standalone fantasy and <b>it lives up to the hype!</b> I am so happy i picked it up. And can we please have more pirate princes who wear eyeliners in YA fantasy?</span>
  <a data-text-id="10057900927105504970" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword">Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword?shelf=addictive">addictive</a>,
