        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2328510238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10046970421605742097"><b>4 “An awesome debut novel” Stars</b><br/><blockquote>
  <i>”Pirates are liars by trade and royals are liars by blood.”</i>
</blockquote><br/><b>This is a fantasy novel in I had a blast while reading it, it was such a fun experience.</b> And recently this has been a struggle since I am shifting my reading preferences towards the contemporary genre. I was so scared to be let down by this book, and I can gladly now say, I was not. The hype surrounding this book is crazy, but it honestly deserves it. <br/><br/>An adventure with my lovely <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/22594701-d-i-a-n-n-a' rel='nofollow noopener'>Monty</a>. I was trash and </span>
  <span id="freeText10046970421605742097" style="display:none"><b>4 “An awesome debut novel” Stars</b><br><blockquote>
  <i>”Pirates are liars by trade and royals are liars by blood.”</i>
</blockquote><br><b>This is a fantasy novel in I had a blast while reading it, it was such a fun experience.</b> And recently this has been a struggle since I am shifting my reading preferences towards the contemporary genre. I was so scared to be let down by this book, and I can gladly now say, I was not. The hype surrounding this book is crazy, but it honestly deserves it. <br><br>An adventure with my lovely <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/22594701-d-i-a-n-n-a" rel="nofollow noopener">Monty</a>. I was trash and kind of left Dianna, but it was still an awesome decision to pick this up.<br><br>I am still in awe of the fact this was a debut novel, it was so refreshing and well crafted. I am looking forward to future works by Alexandra and see how she grows.<br><br><b>The writing was beautiful.</b> I usually tend to have a hard time getting into fantasies, but I was so immersed since the first chapter in this tale. It has a bit of fairy tale whimsical taste to it, which I was definitely fond of. I am also a big fan of the dialogues in between Lira and Elian, literally, it was like looking to people in a ping-pong match. A-D-D-I-C-T-I-N-G. <br><br><b>The world building, captivated me. I want more.</b> I know this is strictly a stand-alone fantasy novel, but I would totally read other stories in this same world (*cough* Sakura and Queen Galina *cough*). I am so overwhelmed by all the possibilities the author has within this novel, all the different lands are rich in possibilities. Even background stories of characters we met in this book, like Madrid. I am telling you, I had to constantly have a break to whisper, holy shit this is so good at the start when we were introduced to the whole siren mechanics and rule. I was <i>mermerazid</i> <s>yeah it should have been sirenized but you get it.</s>.<br> <br><b>The plot/ premise is all I never thought I needed.</b> This was so much fun, and I loved everything about this epic adventure. I will say the ending was a bit disappointing for me. <br><br><b>Characters/ the badass creations of Alexandra Christo’s imagination.</b> It has been a while since I was such a fan of the main characters in a fantasy story <s>okay maybe Penryn from angelfall, but shhhh.</s>. Lira captivated me with her crudeness, pride, and savage attitude. I loved to see how she grew to feel, although I will not lie I was more fan of the ruthless Lira. And Elian was so relatable, his trouble to finding a place to fit in, I got you. I just loved the whole crew, the banter, and the loyalty. They were so fun yet dark and deep at the same time. Oh also, kudos for the Sea Queen imaginary, it was so weird, I loved it. Although my header image was not sexy at all. <s>if you skip ahead you will see my cast for different characters lol.</s><br><br><b>Romance, I was like yes but at the same time not into it.</b> So it has never happened to me before that I enjoy the couple more as individuals than together as a pair. Like I loved them, I loved their tension and banter and everything that lead to more, but when that more arrived I was underwhelmed. #where is the climax? And I was also sad that when Lira found love, her badass edge died quite a bit. Why can’t we have plain mean ruthless main female leads without becoming soft after they fall in love? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Like I truly wonder if I had enjoyed more if she had just killed everyone at the end and rule, like yeah bitches. Maybe not, but I can dream.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I still liked it though, is just that kiss scenes was so plain, I was needy of more after all the tension built. <br><br>In conclusion, this could have been 5 stars but the last 20% left me unsatisfied for some reason. But <b>I definitely recommend it, especially since we don’t get standalone fantasy YA anymore.</b><br><br>1 BONUS: <br>First my giph cast:<br><b>Lira:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1523847275ra/25383842.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>Elian:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474472293ra/20604461.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><b>The Sea Queen:</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1523847275ra/25383843.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>2BONUS:<br><br>Pinterest layout<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1523847319i/25383855._SY540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2243796949" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2243796949" />
    <a title="alana ♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12402009-alana"><img alt="alana ♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599221603p2/12402009.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2243796949?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="alana ♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="alana ♡" href="/user/show/12402009-alana">alana ♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12402009-alana?shelf=retelling">retelling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12402009-alana?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2243796949" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16305728319651614311"><p>
  <em>“Technically, I’m a murderer, but I like to think that’s one of my better qualities.”</em>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <b>Rating: 5/5 stars</b>
  <br/>
</p><p>Sirens. Princes. Betrayals. Oh my!<br/><br/>Have you ever read book before that you could describe as delicious? Because that is the first word that comes to mind when I think about this book. From the very first page until the very last I was hooked.<br/><br/>First of all, if you give me any type of Little Mermaid retelling it's pretty much guaranteed that I will be on board with it. But pair it wi</p></span>
  <span id="freeText16305728319651614311" style="display:none"><p>
  <em>“Technically, I’m a murderer, but I like to think that’s one of my better qualities.”</em>
  <br />
  <br />
  <b>Rating: 5/5 stars</b>
  <br />
</p><p>Sirens. Princes. Betrayals. Oh my!<br /><br />Have you ever read book before that you could describe as delicious? Because that is the first word that comes to mind when I think about this book. From the very first page until the very last I was hooked.<br /><br />First of all, if you give me any type of Little Mermaid retelling it's pretty much guaranteed that I will be on board with it. But pair it with Alexandra Christo's storytelling and you have one of the best YA fantasy/retelling novels I've read in a long time. Second of all, if you give me any type of prince who could be Nikolai Lantsov's long lost brother, who also happens to be a pirate, you better believe I'm dropping everything to read it. Third, if you give me any type of lethal female MC with a tongue sharper than any sword, I'm waiting outside the bookstore weeks before the book comes out. Not really, but you get my point. So it's really a no brainer that this was a five star read for me because it had not one of these, not two, <strong>BUT ALL THREE. </strong><br /><br />The story follows Lira and Elain. Lira, one of the most lethal sirens, also known as the Prince's Bane, happens to be the daughter of the evil Sea Queen. She hunts princes and rips their hearts out every year on her birthday saving the hearts for power. Elain, is the Prince of Midas, who would rather spend his days out in the sea hunting sirens, especially the Prince's Bane,  rather than one day ruling a kingdom.<br /><br />Do you see where this is going?<br /><br />One day Lira and her cousin happen to get on her mothers bad side (as if she even has a good one 😔) and Lira's punishment is to return to her mother with the siren-killer prince's heart. Except Lira is now human, with all of her powers lost. Elian, finds a human girl drowning in the middle of the ocean with no other ship in sight and pulls the girl aboard his ship. She tells Elian she knows the secret to ridding the sea of all sirens. And so begins our story of a dangerous tango between a siren hunter and prince killer.<br /><br />P.S - Sorry if that sucked but I hate writing a synopsis of stories HOWEVER I want you all to see how amazing this one is because I love you all so much.<br /><br />Things you can look forward to in this:<br /><br />-Phenomenal world-building<br />-Banter like you've never read before, seriously, Lira and Elain are a riot together even during serious battle scenes they were still sarcastic assholes to each other, it's amazing<br />-Romance that is <strong>NOT</strong> insta-love, it was the slow burn type of love that fuels my soul<br />-Top notch battle scenes that will have you ripping through the story<br />-Side characters that you are actually invested in<br />-THE  FACT THAT THIS IS A STANDALONE. SO MUCH YES!!!!<br />-Lira's character growth was really fun to read about<br /><br />Also, Elain said in the book to the Sea Queen "<em>sorry, I </em><i>don't speak bitch"</i>, and I'm pretty sure I have never loved a character more in my life.<br /><br />All in all, if you loved the Little Mermaid read this. If you like betrayals, forbidden romance, pirates, sirens, and epic battles READ THIS. Matter of fact, stop reading this review and go get yourself a copy of this, you won't regret it.<br /><br /><br /><a href="https://thebookishchicksblog.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookishchick" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookishchick_/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a></p></span>
  <a data-text-id="16305728319651614311" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2320859663" />
    <a title="Arini" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39722464-arini"><img alt="Arini" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565922259p2/39722464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2320859663?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36120821-to-kill-a-kingdom">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2320859663" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13181459261137334452"><b>1st Reading, March 2018 — 4 Stars<br/>2nd Reading, April 2020 — 3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Honestly, it should be a crime that siren/pirate esque books with as much (if not more) badassery as this one are terribly hard to come by. I need moreee of them in my life! That being said, <b>this book is MARVELOUS</b>. But my reread this time has also brought a couple things into perspective.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve made a mistake. It started with a prince, as most stories do. Once I felt the thrum of his heart beneath my fingers, I couldn’t f</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText13181459261137334452" style="display:none"><b>1st Reading, March 2018 — 4 Stars<br />2nd Reading, April 2020 — 3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />Honestly, it should be a crime that siren/pirate esque books with as much (if not more) badassery as this one are terribly hard to come by. I need moreee of them in my life! That being said, <b>this book is MARVELOUS</b>. But my reread this time has also brought a couple things into perspective.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’ve made a mistake. It started with a prince, as most stories do. Once I felt the thrum of his heart beneath my fingers, I couldn’t forget it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><i>To Kill a Kingdom</i> offers an interesting take on <i>The Little Mermaid</i> tale by turning it into an <b>adventure</b> type of story adorned with themes of friendship, nobel quest, found family, and royal intrigue. <u>It’s dark and brutal and stabby for a YA fantasy</u>. Not to mention, our heroine is everything Ariel isn’t. So for me, that’s a plus.<br /><br />I loved Elian and Lira as individual characters. Whereas <b>Lira</b> is a <b>murderous siren</b> who enjoys ripping the heart out of some prince’s body, <b>Elian</b> is the adventurous, <b>ruthless</b>, and charming <b>pirate</b> who hunts creatures from the likes of Lira and wants nothing to do with becoming a king even though it’s his birthright.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Everyone is a blank canvas, waiting to be filled with the color of discovery.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />The secondary characters (Elian’s crew) are a true blessing. They’re funny, loyal, and protective. And the ‘girl power’ friendship growing between Lira and Madrid is just #goals. <u>The snarky banter and witty dialogues give vibrancy to the perilous task the crew is undertaking</u>. The sea setting is an absolute aesthetic pleasure.<br /><br />Now in my opinion, the mission itself sounds dangerous. But <u>everything about the journey just felt</u> . . . <b>easy</b> with not enough stakes on the line? Even when the crew arrives at their final destination, I was expecting more hurdles, but it’s over in a blink. To add to that, the final battle is a little anticlimactic and quickly turns to mush with Elian and Lira’s PDAs.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I let it all fall away. My mission, my kingdom. The world. They exist somewhere other than in this moment, and now there is only this. Me, my ship, and a girl with oceans in her eyes.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />I’m not picky when it comes to romance in this genre. But Lira and Elian are not doing it for me as a couple. I know people are calling it a slow burn, but I thought it was just so sudden. They have a great <b>PLATONIC</b> relationship development. Then it’s like the book decided to portray them as lovers at the last minute.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="13181459261137334452" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17461038799189732173" style="display:none"><s>this is my first proper review in forever yikes</s><br /><br />I am screaming into the void right now bc lately I’ve only been able to compulsively reread old favs and when I don’t I spend 16 years on A SINGLE BOOK<br /><br />But damn, this book was so bingeable I literally couldn’t stop (this is my form of apologizing to myself for staying up till 2am reading and ruining the next day)<br /><br />Just to tell you how much I loved this book, halfway through I stopped reading so I could make an aesthetic board bc someone gotta<br /><br />Anways, points of awesomeness:<br /><br />-	SIRENS, heart eyes<br />-	A pirate prince <s>who wears eyeliner O H M Y G O O D N E S S</s><br />-	A snarky crew<br />-	<b>ENEMIES TO LOVERS TROPE YES PLEASE</b><br />-	I mean a good portion takes place underwater, how epic is that??<br />-	Kingdoms at war that lead to manipulation, deceit, and death<br />-	A HELL OF A LOT OF SASS (especially the ship yes that’s my shipper heart screaming out of joy)<br /><blockquote>
  <i>Elian says. “When I marry, it won’t be about power.” <br />“What will it be, then?” <br />“Sacrifice.” <br />“You’re right,” I tell him, trying to shake the melancholy from my voice. “Spending a lifetime with you would be a sacrifice.” <br />“Oh?...What would you be losing?” he asks. <br />“If I married you?” I stand to tower above him, pushing away the unraveling thing inside me. “I suppose it would be my mind.” </i>

HOW OFTEN DO WE GET THOSE????<br />-	Its action packed and extremely fast paced, gotta love a book that holds your attention<br />-	And look at that cover <br />-	Honestly my only complaint is that sometimes the dialogue felt a little awkward and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the ending was wrapped up pretty nicely for something that was so brutual <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> but otherwise, an absolutely amazing book<br /><br /><i> “Hearts are power, and if there’s one thing my kind craves more than the ocean, it’s power.”</i><br /><br />4.5 stars!!<br /><br />~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br /><br /><b>

		<td>
		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('0I0ecOw9JpNpzGQM7pAXw5CxGvC1D8UT65NjBbHdz14qu+Ya1nrdthFn6RIjErHpCt0XOOUjKJ5qn3tMBY3JXg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UQFhTZe13mU9VWdMas8UKiMhU264c8f+lLmP1JE0DyurN5knrfIlQEX+6lKnTbIAuU1epuhfKnMVtZedJWQJKw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer4565798772278863623">Alexandra Christo decided to write books when she was four and her teacher told her she couldn’t be a fairy. When she’s not busy making up stories, she can be found organising food crawls over London and binge-watching Korean dramas. <br/><br/>Alexandra has a BA in Creative Writing and currently lives in England with an abundance of cacti (because they’re the only plants she can keep alive). </span>
